## 🧶 Boost Social Media Engagement

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| **Type** | Prompts |
| **Tool** | ChatGPT |
| **Output** | Text |
| **Date** | 2026-05-28 |
| **Views** | 357 |
| **Tags** | Social Media, Content Strategy, Brand Strategy, Strategy |
| **Recommended Tools** | ChatGPT, Gemini, Claude |

> Generate social media engagement strategies with this AI prompt, including conversation starters, comment prompts, storytelling techniques, and community-building tactics.

### Prompt

```
Adopt the role of an expert social media strategist and community architect who has built thriving online communities from scratch across multiple platforms, combining behavioral psychology, viral content mechanics, and authentic relationship-building principles. Your primary objective is to create a comprehensive engagement and community-building strategy that transforms passive followers into active participants and brand advocates through strategic conversation design, emotional resonance, and consistent interaction frameworks in a detailed, actionable format. You operate in an environment where algorithms punish one-way broadcasting, audiences are exhausted by performative content, and authentic connection has become the scarcest commodity. Most creators are trapped in a visibility crisis—posting into the void while competitors with smaller followings generate exponentially more engagement because they've cracked the code of genuine community dynamics. The user needs to break through algorithmic suppression, combat audience fatigue, and create content that people feel compelled to engage with rather than scroll past. Take a deep breath and work on this problem step-by-step.

Analyze the user's current content patterns and audience psychology to identify engagement friction points. Design platform-specific conversation starters that lower the barrier to commenting while creating genuine dialogue opportunities. Develop storytelling frameworks that naturally invite audience participation and shared experiences. Create comment prompt strategies that feel organic rather than manipulative. Build community rituals and recurring engagement formats that train followers to interact consistently. Establish response protocols that amplify engagement momentum. Design content hooks that trigger emotional responses leading to shares and saves. Provide tactics for transforming lurkers into contributors and contributors into community champions.

#INFORMATION ABOUT ME:
My social media platforms: [INSERT YOUR PRIMARY SOCIAL MEDIA PLATFORMS]
My niche/industry: [INSERT YOUR NICHE OR INDUSTRY]
My current engagement rate: [INSERT YOUR AVERAGE ENGAGEMENT RATE OR DESCRIBE CURRENT ENGAGEMENT LEVEL]
My target audience: [INSERT YOUR TARGET AUDIENCE DEMOGRAPHICS AND PSYCHOGRAPHICS]
My content style: [INSERT YOUR CURRENT CONTENT STYLE AND TONE]

MOST IMPORTANT!: Structure your response with clear section headings including Conversation Starters, Comment Prompt Strategies, Storytelling Techniques, Community-Building Tactics, and Implementation Timeline. Provide specific examples and actionable tactics in bullet point format for immediate implementation.
```

### What it does

- Creates a plan to boost interaction on social media content through specific engagement methods.
- Suggests ways to start conversations and prompt comments that make followers want to respond.
- Provides storytelling approaches and community tactics that build consistent follower participation.

### Tips

- Test different conversation starters with your audience to discover which questions spark the most replies, then use this AI prompt regularly to generate fresh variations that keep your community engaged without repeating the same patterns.
- Schedule dedicated time each week to personally respond to comments generated by your posts, as the AI prompt helps create engagement opportunities but building real relationships requires your authentic follow-through and consistent presence.
- Track which storytelling techniques from the AI prompt results drive the highest save and share rates, then create a swipe file of these high-performing formats to guide your content calendar and maximize community growth over time.

### How to use

1. Fill in details about your social media platform, current content type, target audience demographics, and engagement goals when using this AI prompt.
2. Example: "I post on Instagram about fitness for busy moms aged 25-40. I want to increase comments from 5 to 50 per post and build a supportive community around postpartum wellness."

## 🏛️ Build Content Pillars

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| **Type** | Prompts |
| **Tool** | ChatGPT |
| **Output** | Text |
| **Date** | 2026-05-28 |
| **Views** | 169 |
| **Tags** | Social Media, Content Strategy, Brand Strategy, Opportunity Analysis |
| **Recommended Tools** | ChatGPT, Gemini, Claude |

> Create strong content pillars with this AI prompt, including niche-based themes, post ideas, and audience engagement strategies for social media.

### Prompt

```
Adopt the role of an expert content strategist and social media architect who has built viral brands across multiple platforms by identifying authentic voice intersections between creator expertise and audience obsession. Your primary objective is to develop 5 powerful content pillars that form the foundation of a sustainable, engaging social media presence that positions the user as the go-to authority in their niche while creating genuine connection with their audience. Each pillar should represent a distinct facet of their expertise that solves real problems, sparks curiosity, or fulfills emotional needs their audience didn't know they had. Take a deep breath and work on this problem step-by-step.

Analyze the user's niche through the lens of audience pain points, aspirations, and content consumption patterns. Identify the unique angle that differentiates their perspective from competitors. For each of the 5 content pillars, create a compelling pillar name that immediately communicates value, a clear pillar description explaining its strategic purpose, and 6-8 specific post ideas that span educational, entertaining, and inspirational content types. Ensure each pillar can generate endless content variations while maintaining thematic coherence. Balance evergreen content with trend-responsive opportunities. Design pillars that allow the user to showcase different dimensions of their expertise while maintaining brand consistency.

#INFORMATION ABOUT ME:
- My niche/industry: [INSERT YOUR NICHE OR INDUSTRY]
- My expertise/unique perspective: [INSERT YOUR SPECIFIC EXPERTISE OR UNIQUE ANGLE]
- My target audience: [INSERT YOUR TARGET AUDIENCE DETAILS]
- My brand personality/tone: [INSERT YOUR BRAND VOICE AND PERSONALITY]
- My primary social media platforms: [INSERT YOUR MAIN PLATFORMS]

MOST IMPORTANT!: Structure your response with clear headings for each content pillar. Under each pillar, provide the pillar name, strategic purpose, and post ideas in bullet point format for maximum clarity and implementation.
```

### What it does

- Creates five main content themes that support your social media brand strategy.
- Generates multiple post ideas for each content pillar based on your niche.
- Designs AI prompt responses that educate, entertain, or inspire your audience.

### Tips

- Define your niche and expertise clearly before using this AI prompt, as specific details about your industry and unique knowledge will help generate content pillars that truly reflect your brand\
- ,
- ,

## 📬 Build Outreach Automation Playbooks

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| **Type** | Prompts |
| **Tool** | ChatGPT |
| **Output** | Text |
| **Date** | 2026-05-28 |
| **Views** | 14 |
| **Tags** | Outreach, Automation, Lifecycle Messaging |
| **Recommended Tools** | ChatGPT, Gemini, Claude |

> Build outreach automation playbooks with this AI prompt, covering trigger events, message sequencing, personalization logic, and conversion optimization.

### Prompt

```
Design outreach automation playbooks by lifecycle stage:
- New lead nurture
- Trial activation
- Feature adoption
- Inactive re-engagement

For each stage include:
- Trigger conditions
- Message sequence
- Personalization variables
- Exit criteria

# INFORMATION ABOUT ME:
- My audience segments: [INSERT]
- My channels: [INSERT]
- My conversion goals: [INSERT]
- My existing lifecycle events: [INSERT]
```

### What it does

- Creates trigger-based outreach systems tied to lifecycle outcomes.
- Improves conversion quality through stage-specific sequencing.
- Balances automation scale with contextual personalization.

### Tips

- Limit simultaneous campaigns to avoid message overlap.
- Use event quality checks before firing automations.
- Track downstream conversion, not just click metrics.

### How to use

1. Provide segments, events, and goal metrics.
2. Run prompt and deploy sequences in your lifecycle platform.

## 🕸️ Build Social Media Strategies

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| **Type** | Prompts |
| **Tool** | ChatGPT |
| **Output** | Text |
| **Date** | 2026-05-28 |
| **Views** | 77 |
| **Tags** | Social Media, Content Strategy, Brand Strategy, Business Strategy |
| **Recommended Tools** | ChatGPT, Gemini, Claude |

> Create winning social media strategies with this AI prompt, including positioning, content themes, audience analysis, competitor insights, and growth opportunities.

### Prompt

```
Adopt the role of a creative Social Media Strategy Architect, a former magazine editor turned digital pioneer after realizing print's decline forced a pivot to storytelling through screens.

## PHASE 1: DISCOVERY AND ANALYSIS

* What we're doing: Understand your business landscape.
* Approach: Use deep insight to map your business context.
* Actions:
  * Gather business details: niche, target audience, goals.
  * Identify key competitors.
  * Assess unique market positioning.
* Success looks like: Comprehensive business snapshot.

Ready for next? Type "continue"

## PHASE 2: STRATEGIC PLANNING

* What we're doing: Develop a strategic social media framework.
* Approach: Translate business insights into actionable strategies.
* Actions:
  * Define core content themes and pillars.
  * Establish clearly articulated brand voice.
  * Map out growth opportunities.
* Success looks like: A well-defined content and growth blueprint.

Ready for next? Type "continue"

## PHASE 3: IMPLEMENTATION AND OPTIMIZATION

* What we're doing: Activate and refine the social media plan.
* Approach: Execute and iteratively improve through engagement metrics.
* Actions:
  * Launch initial content series based on strategy.
  * Analyze engagement and adjust tactics.
  * Optimize based on real-time feedback and results.
* Success looks like: Improved engagement, audience satisfaction, and measurable growth.

Ready for next? Type "continue"

## PHASE 4: CONTINUOUS ENHANCEMENT (Optional)

* What we're doing: Evolve social media presence over time.
* Approach: Sustain momentum through continual learning and adaptation.
* Actions:
  * Regularly refresh content with emerging trends.
  * Conduct periodic strategy reviews.
  * Cultivate community through interactive experiences.
* Success looks like: A dynamic and thriving social presence that scales.
```

### What it does

- Guides through a social media strategy development process with brand positioning analysis.
- Gathers business details, niche information, target audience profiles, competitor data, and growth goals.
- Delivers a complete social media strategy with positioning framework, content themes, and growth opportunities.

### Tips

- Compile your brand guidelines, past social media analytics, and audience demographic data before using this AI prompt to ensure strategic recommendations align with your existing identity.
- Describe your audience\
- ,

### How to use

1. Run the full prompt and follow the guided questions with detailed answers about your business context.
2. Example: "Business: Online fitness coaching, Niche: Women\

## 🧲 Craft Social Media Posts

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| **Type** | Prompts |
| **Tool** | ChatGPT |
| **Output** | Text |
| **Date** | 2026-05-28 |
| **Views** | 96 |
| **Tags** | Social Media, Content Strategy, Prioritization, Marketing |
| **Recommended Tools** | ChatGPT, Gemini, Claude |

> Create scroll-stopping social media posts with this AI prompt, featuring powerful hooks, clear value delivery, and engagement-driving calls-to-action.

### Prompt

```
# CONTEXT:
Adopt the role of viral content architect. The user operates in an attention economy where they have 0.3 seconds to stop a scrolling thumb among infinite competing content. Algorithms punish boring content with invisibility while rewarding engagement with exponential reach. The user needs to cut through noise created by professional creators, brands with massive budgets, and AI-generated spam. Previous posts disappeared into the void because they looked like everything else. Standard social media advice assumes the user has an existing audience or can afford to post 10 times daily. They need a single post that performs immediately.

# ROLE:
You're a former advertising creative director who got fired for refusing to make boring corporate content, spent two years reverse-engineering viral posts at 3am, and discovered that scroll-stopping isn't about tricks—it's about triggering instant pattern interrupts while delivering genuine value in the first three words. You've obsessively analyzed why some posts with terrible grammar outperform polished content, and you now see social media feeds the way a chess master sees a board—spotting the exact move that breaks through. Your mission: craft a social media post that stops scrolling, delivers value, and triggers engagement. Before any action, think step by step: (1) Identify the pattern interrupt that makes this topic impossible to scroll past, (2) Distill the core value into language a distracted 14-year-old would understand, (3) Design a call-to-action that feels like joining a conversation, not being sold to.

# RESPONSE GUIDELINES:
This task requires creating structured text formatted for social media consumption. The response should be organized as follows:

**Section 1 - The Hook (Goal: Stop the scroll within 0.3 seconds)**
- Open with a pattern interrupt that violates expectations
- Use the first 3-7 words to create cognitive dissonance or curiosity
- Avoid generic openings that blend into feeds

**Section 2 - Value Delivery (Goal: Justify why they stopped scrolling)**
- Translate the topic into clear, simple language
- Use short sentences and line breaks for mobile readability
- Deliver one concrete insight or perspective shift
- Make it skimmable while rewarding full reading

**Section 3 - Call-to-Action (Goal: Convert attention into engagement)**
- Frame participation as contribution, not compliance
- Ask questions that people actually want to answer
- Make sharing feel like adding value to their own audience

The response should feel like a conversation, not a broadcast. Each element must earn its place—no filler, no fluff, no corporate speak.

# TASK CRITERIA:

**Essential Requirements:**
1. The hook must create immediate pattern disruption—no "Hey guys" or "I've been thinking about" openings
2. Use line breaks strategically to create visual breathing room and emphasize key points
3. Write at an 8th-grade reading level maximum—complexity kills engagement
4. The entire post must be skimmable in 5 seconds while rewarding 30-second deep reading
5. Call-to-action must feel organic, not tacked on

**Strict Limitations:**
- Do NOT use corporate jargon, buzzwords, or marketing speak
- Do NOT write hooks that require context to understand
- Do NOT create calls-to-action that feel like homework ("Tag 3 friends!")
- Do NOT use adjectives and adverbs unless absolutely necessary for clarity
- Do NOT assume the audience knows anything about the topic
- Do NOT make the post about you unless your experience directly serves the value

**Focus Areas:**
- Prioritize immediate comprehension over cleverness
- Optimize for mobile reading (short lines, visual breaks)
- Design for the algorithm (comments > shares > likes in value)
- Make the first sentence work even if it's the only thing someone reads

# INFORMATION ABOUT ME:
- My topic: [INSERT TOPIC]
- My target audience: [INSERT TARGET AUDIENCE]
- My desired engagement type: [INSERT DESIRED ENGAGEMENT - comments/shares/saves]

# RESPONSE FORMAT:
Provide the social media post in clean, formatted text with strategic line breaks. Structure it as:

**[The complete scroll-stopping post ready to copy and paste]**

Followed by:

**Why This Works:**
- Brief bullet points explaining the psychological triggers used
- Specific elements that optimize for algorithm performance

Do not use tables, scores, or XML formatting. Present the post exactly as it should appear on the social media platform.
```

### What it does

- Creates engaging social media content that captures attention with a strong opening hook.
- Delivers clear value using simple language that readers can easily understand.
- Ends with a call-to-action that encourages audience interaction through comments or shares.

### Tips

- Test different hook styles with your AI prompt by asking it to generate multiple opening lines, then choose the one that best captures attention and matches your brand voice.
- Analyze your top-performing posts before using this AI prompt to identify patterns in what resonates with your audience, helping you provide better context for more targeted results.
- After generating your post, ask the AI prompt to create 3-5 conversation-starting questions as comment replies to boost engagement when your audience starts responding.

---

## 🧬 Create Athletic Grid Advertisements

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| **Type** | Prompts |
| **Tool** | Nano Banana |
| **Output** | Text |
| **Date** | 2026-05-28 |
| **Views** | 28 |
| **Tags** | Social Media, Brand Strategy, Photography, Advertising |
| **Recommended Tools** | Nano Banana |

> Create dynamic athletic product advertisements with this AI prompt, featuring grid layouts, motion shots, fabric details, and lifestyle branding elements.

### Prompt

```
{
  "Objective": "Create a dynamic 2×3 grid advertisement for [PRODUCT NAME], showcasing movement, material innovation, and everyday athletic lifestyle.",
  "Canvas": {
    "Aspect_Ratio": "4:5",
    "Grid_Structure": "2×3 equal panels",
    "Orientation": "Portrait",
    "Use_Case": [
      "Fitness brand social media",
      "E-commerce product galleries",
      "Digital performance ads",
      "Athletic lifestyle campaigns"
    ]
  },
  "Panels": [
    {
      "Panel_Number": 1,
      "Title": "Hero Apparel Look",
      "Description": "Studio-style hero shot of [PRODUCT NAME] worn by an athlete.",
      "Visual_Details": {
        "Lighting": "Soft directional studio lighting",
        "Background": "Neutral gradient or concrete tone",
        "Focus": "Fit, silhouette, and logo placement",
        "Mood": ["Strength", "Confidence", "Performance"]
      }
    },
    {
      "Panel_Number": 2,
      "Title": "Dynamic Motion",
      "Description": "Athlete in motion performing [ATHLETIC DISCIPLINE: signature explosive movement].",
      "Visual_Details": {
        "Lighting": "Natural daylight",
        "Motion": "Frozen action with crisp detail",
        "Mood": ["Energy", "Power", "Momentum"]
      }
    },
    {
      "Panel_Number": 3,
      "Title": "Fabric Technology",
      "Description": "Macro close-up of fabric texture stretched or flexed during movement.",
      "Visual_Details": {
        "Focus": "Breathability, weave detail, and material performance",
        "Depth_of_Field": "Shallow and precise",
        "Mood": ["Innovation", "Engineering"]
      }
    },
    {
      "Panel_Number": 4,
      "Title": "Everyday Training",
      "Description": "Athlete training in [ATHLETIC DISCIPLINE: typical training environment].",
      "Visual_Details": {
        "Lighting": "Balanced natural light",
        "Environment": "Urban or outdoor fitness space",
        "Mood": ["Consistency", "Lifestyle"]
      }
    },
    {
      "Panel_Number": 5,
      "Title": "Comfort & Fit Detail",
      "Description": "Close-up of construction details — waistband, seams, stitching, or closure system.",
      "Visual_Details": {
        "Focus": "Construction quality and comfort engineering",
        "Mood": ["Precision", "Durability"]
      }
    },
    {
      "Panel_Number": 6,
      "Title": "Post-Workout Calm",
      "Description": "Athlete in [ATHLETIC DISCIPLINE: recovery or cool-down moment].",
      "Visual_Details": {
        "Lighting": "Warm natural light",
        "Mood": ["Recovery", "Balance", "Well-being"]
      }
    }
  ],
  "Branding": {
    "Product_Name": "[PRODUCT NAME]",
    "Brand_Personality": "Driven, modern, performance-focused",
    "Color_Palette": "[COLOR PALETTE]",
    "Logo_Presentation": "Minimal, performance-oriented placement"
  },
  "Visual_Style": {
    "Style_Keywords": [
      "Performance sports advertising",
      "High realism",
      "Minimalist athletic aesthetic",
      "Clean compositions",
      "Premium fitness branding"
    ]
  },
  "Camera_And_Lighting": {
    "Photography_Type": "Professional sports and lifestyle photography",
    "Shot_Types": [
      "Hero apparel shot",
      "Action shot",
      "Macro material detail",
      "Lifestyle training scene"
    ],
    "Lighting_Style": "Natural daylight mixed with soft studio fill",
    "Exposure": "Balanced with crisp highlights",
    "Shadows": "Defined yet clean"
  },
  "Mood_Keywords": [
    "Strong",
    "Focused",
    "Energetic",
    "Modern",
    "Resilient",
    "Balanced"
  ],
  "Negative_Prompt": [
    "Baggy or ill-fitting clothing",
    "Low-quality fabric appearance",
    "Motion blur on subject",
    "Distracting backgrounds",
    "Oversaturated colors",
    "Cheap logo placement",
    "CGI or cartoon style",
    "Watermarks",
    "Text overlays"
  ]
}
```

### What it does

- Creates a 2×3 grid AI image showcasing athletic apparel through six distinct panels featuring hero shots, action sequences, and fabric details.
- Generates professional sports photography scenes that highlight product performance, material innovation, and lifestyle training moments.
- Produces a cohesive fitness brand advertisement with balanced lighting, clean compositions, and premium athletic aesthetic across all panels.

### Tips

- Choose a specific athletic discipline that matches your product\
- ,
- ,

### How to use

1. Step 1: Attach your logo / image.

## 🫧 Create Beverage Advertisements

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| **Type** | Prompts |
| **Tool** | Nano Banana |
| **Output** | Text |
| **Date** | 2026-05-28 |
| **Views** | 508 |
| **Tags** | Campaigns, Social Media, Brand Strategy, Photography |
| **Recommended Tools** | Nano Banana |

> Create vibrant beverage advertisements with this AI prompt, featuring product photography, lifestyle scenes, splash effects, and modern urban branding elements.

### Prompt

```
{
  "Objective": "Create a vibrant 3×2 advertisement for [PRODUCT NAME] [BEVERAGE TYPE], presenting an everyday soft drink with a stylish, high-quality background and energetic lifestyle aesthetic.",
  "Canvas": {
    "Aspect_Ratio": "16:9",
    "Grid_Structure": "3×2 equal panels",
    "Orientation": "Landscape",
    "Use_Case": [
      "Beverage marketing campaigns",
      "Social media ads",
      "Billboard displays",
      "Retail promotional visuals"
    ]
  },
  "Product_Description": {
    "Category": "Carbonated Soft Drink",
    "Packaging_Type": "Slim aluminum can with bold graphic design",
    "Flavor": "Classic cola with citrus twist",
    "Features": [
      "Cold refreshing carbonation",
      "Matte-finish can design",
      "Bold logo typography",
      "Everyday grab-and-go drink"
    ]
  },
  "Background_Design": {
    "Environment": "Modern urban rooftop setting",
    "Surface": "Concrete slab with subtle texture",
    "Accent_Elements": [
      "Ice cubes scattered around can",
      "Light water droplets",
      "Soft sunset sky gradient",
      "Minimal city skyline silhouette"
    ],
    "Lighting": "Golden hour sunlight with cool reflective highlights",
    "Mood": ["Cool", "Refreshing", "Modern"]
  },
  "Panels": [
    {
      "Panel_Number": 1,
      "Title": "Hero Can Shot",
      "Description": "[PRODUCT NAME] can centered upright with condensation droplets.",
      "Visual_Details": {
        "Camera_Angle": "Low-angle for bold presence",
        "Mood": ["Bold", "Refreshing"]
      }
    },
    {
      "Panel_Number": 2,
      "Title": "Open & Fizz Moment",
      "Description": "Close-up of soda can being opened with visible fizz.",
      "Visual_Details": {
        "Lighting": "Backlit to highlight carbonation",
        "Mood": ["Dynamic", "Crisp"]
      }
    },
    {
      "Panel_Number": 3,
      "Title": "Ice & Splash Detail",
      "Description": "Soda splash with ice cubes frozen mid-air.",
      "Visual_Details": {
        "Lighting": "High-speed capture lighting",
        "Mood": ["Energetic", "Cold"]
      }
    },
    {
      "Panel_Number": 4,
      "Title": "Lifestyle Moment",
      "Description": "Young adult holding soda during casual rooftop hangout.",
      "Visual_Details": {
        "Lighting": "Warm sunset glow",
        "Mood": ["Relaxed", "Social"]
      }
    },
    {
      "Panel_Number": 5,
      "Title": "Can Texture Close-Up",
      "Description": "Macro shot of aluminum texture and condensation.",
      "Visual_Details": {
        "Depth_of_Field": "Ultra-shallow",
        "Mood": ["Fresh", "Cold"]
      }
    },
    {
      "Panel_Number": 6,
      "Title": "Graphic Brand Finish",
      "Description": "Can centered against bold color-block sunset gradient.",
      "Visual_Details": {
        "Lighting": "Clean studio lighting",
        "Mood": ["Modern", "Eye-catching"]
      }
    }
  ],
  "Branding": {
    "Product_Name": "[PRODUCT NAME]",
    "Brand_Personality": "Energetic, bold, youthful",
    "Color_Palette": [COLOR PALETTE],
    "Typography": "Bold modern sans-serif"
  },
  "Visual_Style": {
    "Style_Keywords": [
      "Modern beverage photography",
      "Urban lifestyle aesthetic",
      "High realism",
      "Dynamic splash capture",
      "Bold color composition"
    ]
  },
  "Camera_And_Lighting": {
    "Photography_Type": "Professional product and lifestyle photography",
    "Shot_Types": [
      "Hero product shot",
      "Macro condensation detail",
      "High-speed splash capture",
      "Lifestyle rooftop scene"
    ],
    "Lighting_Style": "Golden hour with controlled highlights",
    "Exposure": "Vibrant and balanced",
    "Shadows": "Soft but defined"
  },
  "Mood_Keywords": [
    "Refreshing",
    "Energetic",
    "Cool",
    "Bold",
    "Social",
    "Modern"
  ],
  "Negative_Prompt": [
    "Flat soda",
    "Dented can",
    "Messy background",
    "Overexposed highlights",
    "Plastic-looking liquid",
    "Cartoon style",
    "Low-resolution detail",
    "Watermarks",
    "Text overlays"
  ]
}
```

### What it does

- Creates a vibrant 3×2 grid AI image advertisement showcasing a carbonated soft drink across six distinct panels in 16:9 format.
- Generates professional product photography scenes including hero shots, fizz moments, ice splashes, and lifestyle scenarios on an urban rooftop.
- Produces high-quality beverage marketing visuals with golden hour lighting, modern aesthetics, and energetic mood for social media and billboard use.

### Tips

- Choose a product name and beverage type that reflects your brand identity, such as "Zest Cola" for a citrus-forward drink or "Urban Rush Energy Soda" for a bold lifestyle brand.
- Select a color palette that matches your product\

## 🦌 Create Cinematic Environmental Portraits

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| **Type** | Prompts |
| **Tool** | Nano Banana |
| **Output** | Text |
| **Date** | 2026-05-28 |
| **Views** | 32 |
| **Tags** | Photography, Marketing, Content Strategy, Cinematic |
| **Recommended Tools** | Nano Banana |

> Generate hyper-realistic portrait photography with this AI prompt, featuring customizable environment, outfit, lighting, and cinematic depth using professional camera settings.

### Prompt

```
{
  "prompt": "Hyper-realistic environmental portrait of a stylish young woman standing in a dense [ENVIRONMENT]. She is wearing [OUTFIT STYLE]. She stands with a confident posture, leaning slightly forward, with her right hand resting naturally on a nearby vertical element in the scene. The lighting is soft and diffused with dappled sunlight filtering through the surroundings, highlighting the texture of the environment and her clothing. The background features a deep cinematic depth of field (bokeh) with rich natural tones and organic undergrowth. Shot on Sony A7R IV, 35mm lens at f/1.8, high contrast, matte finish, sharp focus on subject, 8k resolution.",
  "negative_prompt": "cartoon, anime, 3d render, illustration, painting, low quality, blurry, distorted face, bad anatomy, extra fingers, missing limbs, text, watermark, neon colors, overexposed, harsh lighting, bright artificial light, makeup smudge, messy hair",
  "metadata": {
    "subject": "Woman",
    "hair_color": "Brown",
    "outfit": ["[OUTFIT STYLE — list individual pieces]"],
    "environment": "[ENVIRONMENT]",
    "lighting": "Natural soft daylight, dappled",
    "camera_settings": "35mm, f/1.8, Depth of Field",
    "style": "Cinematic, Minimalist, Photorealistic"
  }
}
```

### What it does

- Generates a hyper-realistic AI image of a stylish woman posed confidently in a natural environment with customizable outfit and setting options.
- Uses cinematic lighting techniques with soft dappled sunlight to create depth and highlight textures in both subject and surroundings.
- Produces professional photography-quality output with sharp focus, bokeh background, and 8k resolution using specified camera settings.

### Tips

- Choose a natural environment that complements the mood you want, such as bamboo forest for calm elegance or urban jungle for edgy vibes, and match the outfit style accordingly like flowing linen dress or structured leather jacket.
- Consider how the vertical element she leans on relates to your chosen environment, such as a tree trunk in woodland settings or a weathered post in industrial spaces, to create natural interaction in your AI image.
- Use the JSON prompt to guide the AI in creating a cinematic portrait, and experiment with contrasting outfit textures against the environment like soft knits in rough bark forests or sleek fabrics in overgrown urban scenes.

---

| Field | Value |

| **Recommended Tools** | Nano Banana |

> Create photorealistic tablet mockups with this AI prompt, featuring cinematic lighting, perspective warping, screen replacement, and futuristic presentation styling.

### Prompt

```
{
  "task": "cinematic_tablet_screen_replacement",
  "input": {
    "user_uploaded_image": "PLACEHOLDER_FOR_UPLOADED_IMAGE",
    "auto_fit_to_screen": true,
    "preserve_aspect_ratio": true,
    "center_crop_if_needed": true
  },
  "scene": {
    "composition": "floating tablet held by [HOLDER]",
    "camera_angle": "angled perspective, slight right tilt",
    "device_orientation": "landscape",
    "background": "[BACKGROUND]",
    "vibe": "high-tech futuristic presentation"
  },
  "screen_integration": {
    "replace_existing_screen_content": true,
    "remove_existing_UI_text": true,
    "apply_strong_perspective_warp": true,
    "match_tablet_rotation_angle": true,
    "respect_bezel_boundaries": true,
    "simulate_real_glass_depth": true,
    "apply_subtle_blue_light_reflection": true,
    "add_soft_screen_glow": true,
    "avoid_flat_overlay_effect": true
  },
  "lighting": {
    "style": "dramatic cinematic lighting",
    "key_light": "cool blue directional light from front",
    "rim_light": "subtle metallic highlights on tablet edges",
    "shadow_intensity": "medium contrast",
    "color_grade": "cool high-contrast tech tone"
  },
  "realism_rules": {
    "preserve_robot_arm_details": true,
    "maintain_metallic_reflections": true,
    "no_device_warping": true,
    "no_screen_spill_over_bezel": true,
    "maintain_depth_and_shadow_consistency": true
  },
  "output": {
    "style": "ultra photorealistic cinematic render",
    "resolution": "high resolution",
    "detail_level": "advertising quality",
    "no_added_text": true
  }
}
```

### What it does

- Replaces the screen content on a tablet device with a user-uploaded AI image while maintaining realistic perspective and proportions.
- Applies cinematic lighting effects with blue tones, glass reflections, and screen glow to create a high-tech futuristic presentation.
- Generates an ultra-photorealistic AI image showing the tablet held at an angled perspective with dramatic shadows and metallic highlights.

### Tips

- Upload your app interface, website design, or product dashboard in high-resolution for the AI image to display naturally on the tablet screen.
- Choose a holder that matches your brand story, such as a robotic arm for tech products or human hands for lifestyle apps.
- Select a background that complements your content, like a minimalist studio for professional software or a futuristic cityscape for gaming apps.

```
        "details": "bright, patterned, summery"
      }
    },
    "face": {

      "makeup": {
        "cheeks": "soft blush on cheeks and nose",

        "overall": "subtle and identical to reference"
      }
    }

  },
  "background": {

    "elements": [],
    "atmosphere": "vibrant, summery, high-contrast",
    "lighting": "strong natural sunlight"
  }
}
```

### What it does

- Generates an AI image of a young woman in editorial fashion style wearing an oversized cardigan, patterned headscarf, and large tortoise-shell sunglasses.
- Creates a warm summer portrait with intense backlit sunlight, lens flares, and high-contrast lighting against a bright blue sky.
- Features an animal companion resting on her shoulder while preserving natural makeup details and wind-blown layered hair.

### Tips

- Choose a fashion aesthetic that defines your AI image prompt style, such as bohemian for earthy tones and flowing fabrics, vintage for retro patterns and muted colors, or modern minimalist for clean lines and neutral palettes.
- Select an animal companion that complements the editorial fashion vibe, like a colorful parrot for tropical energy, a sleek cat for sophisticated elegance, or a small bird for delicate charm.
- Use the JSON prompt to guide the AI in creating a cohesive color story where the cardigan and headscarf share the same aesthetic palette, ensuring your fashion editorial AI image maintains visual harmony.

### How to use

1. Step 1: Attach your logo / image.

```
{

      }
```

```
    "Style_Keywords": [
      "Gaming hardware advertising",
      "High realism",
      "Dark premium aesthetic",
      "Minimalist tech composition",
      "E-sports inspired"
    ]

  "Camera_And_Lighting": {
    "Photography_Type": "Professional commercial product photography",

      "Hero product shot",
      "Macro engineering detail",
      "Lifestyle gaming scene"
    ],

    "Fast",
```

- Define a specific PERFORMANCE FEATURE for the macro shot in panel 2, like optical sensor technology, mechanical switch construction, or premium braided cable detail, to showcase what makes your product technically superior.

```

      "Restaurant poster",

      "Text": "[BRAND NAME]",

      "Style": "Bold modern serif",

      "Text": "Ignite Your Cravings.",
      "Placement": "Below brand name",
      "Style": "Clean thin sans-serif",

    }

      "Warm restaurant ambiance",
      "Texture-focused lighting",
      "Appetite appeal composition"
    ]
  },
  "Camera_Settings": {
    "Lens_Look": "85mm food photography look",
    "Angle": "Eye-level or slight low angle",

    "Juicy",
    "Savory",
    "Bold",
    "Warm",
    "Inviting",
    "Crave-worthy"
  ],
  "Negative_Prompt": [
    "Dry meat texture",
    "Flat lighting",
    "Soggy bun",
    "Messy ingredient spill",
    "Overexposed highlights",
    "Cartoon style",

    "Watermarks",
    "Text artifacts"
  ]
}
```

```
{
```

```
    "main_prompt": "Shot on a Canon EOS R5 with an RF 85mm f/1.2L USM lens, a striking figure stands with confident allure in a [ENVIRONMENT SETTING], poised in a captivating '[POSE STYLE]'. Soft, diffused golden hour light streams dramatically through translucent sheer linen curtains, bathing her form in a painterly glow and creating a perfect, creamy bokeh that softens the background of exposed brick and minimalist decor.",
    "subject_details": {
      "outfit": "[OUTFIT DESCRIPTION] with a fluid, delicate sheen.",

    },
    "face_consistency_instruction": "Maintain 100% face consistency with reference image."
  }
}
```

- Generates a high-fashion portrait AI image shot with professional camera settings and golden hour lighting.
- Creates hyper-realistic skin textures and details while maintaining face consistency with a reference photo.
- Produces an editorial-style AI image with warm tones, creamy bokeh, and minimalist background elements.

### Tips

- Select an environment setting that complements your creative vision, such as a sunlit loft apartment for modern elegance or a vintage studio for timeless appeal.
- Choose a pose style that conveys the desired emotion, like a relaxed lean against a wall for casual confidence or a dynamic turn toward the camera for editorial drama.
- Describe the outfit with specific fabric details and colors that work with golden hour lighting, such as a flowing silk slip dress in champagne tones or a structured linen blazer in warm earth colors.

### Prompt

```
{
  "task": "high_end_beauty_product_photography",
  "input": {
    "product_image": "UPLOAD_YOUR_PRODUCT_IMAGE_HERE"
  },
  "composition": {
    "framing": "tight close-up portrait",
    "crop": "head and upper shoulders",
    "angle": "front-facing, eye-level",
    "aspect_ratio": "4:5",
    "focus": "sharp focus on face and product, shallow depth of field background"
  },
  "subject": {
    "gender": "female",
    "ethnicity": "[MODEL LOOK]",
    "age_range": "mid 20s",
    "beauty_description": "extremely beautiful, natural features consistent with [MODEL LOOK], symmetrical face, high cheekbones, soft jawline",
    "eyes": "striking eye color natural to [MODEL LOOK], crystal clear catchlights",
    "lips": "naturally full, hydrated gloss finish",
    "skin": {
      "texture": "ultra detailed pores, realistic micro texture",
      "finish": "[SKIN FINISH]",
      "enhancement": "subtle skin perfection without plastic smoothing",
      "quality": "8K hyperreal skin detail with subsurface scattering"
    },
    "hair": "wet slicked-back hair, natural hair color consistent with [MODEL LOOK], natural shine",
    "expression": "soft kissy lips expression (subtle pout), relaxed but confident"
  },
  "product_placement": {
    "position": "held horizontally covering one eye",
    "orientation": "label facing camera fully readable",
    "integration": "natural hand grip, realistic finger pressure and shadow interaction",
    "lighting_interaction": "realistic reflections and moisture droplets on product surface"
  },
  "lighting": {
    "type": "soft diffused beauty lighting",
    "setup": "large frontal softbox + subtle rim light for hair separation",
    "skin_highlights": "controlled glossy highlights on cheekbones and forehead",
    "shadow_style": "very soft minimal shadows"
  },
  "background": {
    "color": "[BACKGROUND TONE]",
    "texture": "smooth seamless studio backdrop",
    "blur": "slight creamy blur"
  },
  "camera": {
    "lens": "85mm prime lens",
    "aperture": "f/2.0",
    "resolution": "8K ultra high resolution",
    "color_profile": "natural skin tones, commercial beauty grade"
  },
  "render_style": {
    "photorealism_level": "extreme",
    "detail_level": "ultra high",
    "finish": "luxury skincare campaign aesthetic",
    "avoid": "cartoon, CGI look, plastic skin, over-smoothing, artificial textures"
  }
}
```

### What it does

- Generates a high-end beauty product AI image with a female model holding the product at eye level in a tight portrait composition.
- Creates hyperrealistic skin texture with 8K detail while maintaining natural beauty through soft diffused lighting and shallow depth of field.
- Produces a luxury skincare campaign aesthetic where the product label remains clearly visible and naturally integrated with the model\

### Tips

- Upload your product image in high-resolution on transparent background to ensure the label remains sharp and readable when positioned over the model\

### Prompt

```
luxury editorial portrait of an elegant [SUBJECT IDENTITY] standing beside a [ANIMAL COMPANION] in [ENVIRONMENT SETTING], cinematic fashion photography subject (woman): [FULL SUBJECT DESCRIPTION] clothing and jewelry: [WARDROBE AND ADORNMENT] prop (weapon): [CEREMONIAL PROP DESCRIPTION] animal: [ANIMAL DESCRIPTION] environment: [ENVIRONMENT DETAIL] lighting: dramatic natural sunlight cutting through the jungle canopy, warm highlights on the woman's skin and gold jewelry, deep emerald shadows in the background creating contrast color palette: rich jungle greens, warm golden skin tones, metallic gold highlights, earthy browns of the leopard, deep teal and emerald foliage composition: woman positioned slightly left of center with the spear rising vertically beside her, leopard positioned to the right with its head level with the woman's shoulder, dense foliage framing both subjects style: high fashion editorial photography, exotic jungle aesthetic, cinematic lighting, luxury magazine cover style camera: 85mm lens, shallow depth of field, sharp focus on woman and leopard, soft blurred foliage behind ultra detailed, cinematic lighting, high fashion editorial, natural textures, vibrant colors --chaos 30 --ar 3:4 --sref 3775199334 1360520854 3015451063 --p
```

- Generates a cinematic magazine-style portrait with shallow depth of field that keeps the subject and animal in sharp focus.

### Tips

- Describe wardrobe details that complement the environment setting, like gold-threaded silk robes for jungle scenes or leather adorned with feathers for savanna backdrops.
- Choose ceremonial props and animal descriptions that tell a cohesive story, matching ornate spears with regal big cats or carved staffs with exotic birds to enhance the luxury editorial feel of your AI image.

## 🫧 Create Luxury Product Advertisement Panels

| Field | Value |
|---|---|

> Create luxury product advertisements with this AI prompt, featuring multi-panel layouts, architectural photography, wellness branding, and premium visual storytelling elements.

### Prompt

```
{
  "Objective": "Create a premium 3×2 luxury advertisement for the [PRODUCT NAME] [PRODUCT TYPE], emphasizing clean air technology, architectural design presence, and modern wellness living.",
  "Canvas": {
    "Aspect_Ratio": "4:5",
    "Grid_Structure": "3×2 equal panels",
    "Orientation": "Portrait",
    "Use_Case": [
      "Luxury wellness campaigns",
      "Smart home marketing",
      "Interior design advertising",
      "Social media premium branding"
    ]
  },
  "Product_Description": {
    "Category": "Luxury [PRODUCT TYPE]",
    "Material": "Matte ceramic outer shell with brushed aluminum core",
    "Features": [
      "360° HEPA filtration",
      "Real-time air quality display",
      "Whisper-quiet operation",
      "AI adaptive purification system",
      "Ambient halo light indicator"
    ]
  },
  "Panels": [
    {
      "Panel_Number": 1,
      "Title": "Hero Sculptural Presence",
      "Description": "[PRODUCT NAME] positioned in a minimalist concrete and glass living space.",
      "Visual_Details": {
        "Lighting": "Soft natural daylight from large windows",
        "Mood": ["Architectural", "Refined", "Minimal"]
      }
    },
    {
      "Panel_Number": 2,
      "Title": "Air Flow Visualization",
      "Description": "Subtle visual effect showing purified airflow rising around device.",
      "Visual_Details": {
        "Lighting": "Soft diffused glow",
        "Mood": ["Clean", "Advanced"]
      }
    },
    {
      "Panel_Number": 3,
      "Title": "Material Detail",
      "Description": "Macro close-up of ceramic finish and precision vent design.",
      "Visual_Details": {
        "Depth_of_Field": "Ultra-shallow, crisp",
        "Mood": ["Craftsmanship", "Premium"]
      }
    },
    {
      "Panel_Number": 4,
      "Title": "Wellness Lifestyle",
      "Description": "Adult practicing yoga or reading in purified modern space.",
      "Visual_Details": {
        "Lighting": "Bright natural daylight",
        "Mood": ["Calm", "Healthy", "Balanced"]
      }
    },
    {
      "Panel_Number": 5,
      "Title": "Smart Display Detail",
      "Description": "Close-up of minimal digital air-quality interface.",
      "Visual_Details": {
        "Mood": ["Intelligent", "Innovative"]
      }
    },
    {
      "Panel_Number": 6,
      "Title": "Night Ambient Mode",
      "Description": "Purifier glowing softly in dim modern interior.",
      "Visual_Details": {
        "Lighting": "Low-key ambient halo light",
        "Mood": ["Serene", "Quiet luxury"]
      }
    }
  ],
  "Branding": {
    "Product_Name": "[PRODUCT NAME]",
    "Brand_Personality": "Pure, intelligent, architectural",
    "Color_Palette": [COLOR PALETTE],
    "Typography": "Thin modern sans-serif"
  },
  "Visual_Style": {
    "Style_Keywords": [
      "Luxury wellness advertising",
      "Architectural interior photography",
      "High realism",
      "Minimalist composition",
      "Smart home aesthetic"
    ]
  },
  "Camera_And_Lighting": {
    "Photography_Type": "Professional architectural and product photography",
    "Shot_Types": [
      "Wide interior hero shot",
      "Macro material detail",
      "Lifestyle wellness scene"
    ],
    "Lighting_Style": "Soft natural daylight with subtle ambient fill",
    "Exposure": "Bright and clean",
    "Shadows": "Soft and architectural"
  },
  "Mood_Keywords": [
    "Pure",
    "Calm",
    "Modern",
    "Clean",
    "Refined",
    "Healthy"
  ],
  "Negative_Prompt": [
    "Dusty environment",
    "Cheap plastic look",
    "Cluttered room",
    "Harsh lighting",
    "Overexposed highlights",
    "Cartoon style",
    "Low-resolution textures",
    "Watermarks",
    "Text overlays"
  ]
}
```

### What it does

- Generates a luxury 3×2 panel AI image advertisement showcasing an air purifier in premium architectural settings.
- Creates six distinct scenes ranging from hero product shots to lifestyle wellness moments with professional lighting.
- Produces high-resolution AI images emphasizing clean design, smart technology features, and modern minimalist aesthetics.

### Tips

- Choose a specific product name and type that matches your brand, such as "AeroZen Air Purifier" or "LuxeBreath Humidifier", to personalize the AI image prompt for your campaign.
- Select a cohesive color palette that reflects your brand identity, like soft whites and sage greens for wellness or charcoal and rose gold for modern luxury, ensuring consistency across all six panels.
- Use the JSON prompt to guide the AI in creating a premium multi-panel advertisement that showcases your product from hero shots to lifestyle scenes.

### How to use

1. Step 1: Attach your logo / image.

> Create luxury product advertisements with this AI prompt, featuring premium craftsmanship, cinematic lighting, minimal design, and sophisticated brand storytelling elements.

### Prompt

```
{
  "Objective": "Create a powerful single-frame hero product advertisement for the [BRAND NAME] [ACCESSORY TYPE], emphasizing premium craftsmanship, minimal elegance, and strong visual focus.",
  "Canvas": {
    "Aspect_Ratio": "3:4",
    "Grid_Structure": "1×1 hero layout",
    "Orientation": "Portrait",
    "Use_Case": [
      "Luxury product poster",
      "Instagram fashion ad",
      "Website hero section",
      "E-commerce premium listing"
    ]
  },
  "Product_Description": {
    "Category": "Premium Leather Wallet",
    "Material": "Full-grain Italian leather",
    "Color": "Deep espresso brown",
    "Features": [
      "Hand-stitched edges",
      "Slim modern profile",
      "Multiple card slots",
      "Embossed logo detail"
    ]
  },
  "Composition": {
    "Placement": "Wallet centered vertically and horizontally",
    "Surface": "Matte dark marble slab",
    "Background": "Soft gradient charcoal-to-warm brown backdrop",
    "Camera_Angle": "Slight 45-degree angle to show depth",
    "Depth_of_Field": "Shallow to isolate product"
  },
  "Lighting": {
    "Style": "Cinematic soft spotlight from upper left",
    "Highlights": "Subtle rim light accentuating leather texture",
    "Shadows": "Soft grounding shadow beneath product",
    "Mood": ["Refined", "Elegant", "Confident"]
  },
  "Typography": {
    "Brand_Name": {
      "Text": "[BRAND NAME]",
      "Placement": "Top center",
      "Style": "Elegant high-fashion serif with wide letter spacing",
      "Color": "Soft gold or warm ivory"
    },
    "Tagline": {
      "Text": "Crafted for the Modern Gentleman",
      "Placement": "Below brand name, above product",
      "Style": "Thin minimalist sans-serif",
      "Color": "Muted beige"
    }
  },
  "Visual_Style": {
    "Style_Keywords": [
      "Luxury product photography",
      "Minimal editorial aesthetic",
      "High realism",
      "Premium material focus",
      "Cinematic lighting"
    ]
  },
  "Camera_Settings": {
    "Lens_Look": "85mm product photography",
    "Focus": "Sharp on logo and stitching",
    "Exposure": "Balanced with rich shadows"
  },
  "Mood_Keywords": [
    "Timeless",
    "Confident",
    "Minimal",
    "Premium",
    "Sophisticated"
  ],
  "Negative_Prompt": [
    "Cheap synthetic leather look",
    "Overexposed highlights",
    "Flat lighting",
    "Cluttered background",
    "Low-resolution texture",
    "Cartoon style",
    "Watermarks",
    "Text artifacts"
  ]
}
```

### What it does

- Generates a luxury product advertisement AI image showcasing a premium leather wallet in portrait format.
- Uses cinematic lighting and shallow depth to highlight craftsmanship details like hand-stitched edges and embossed logo.
- Creates a minimal editorial composition with elegant typography on a dark marble surface for high-end marketing use.

### Tips

- Choose your accessory type and material that match your brand identity, such as leather wallets, watches, or sunglasses with specific textures like Italian leather or brushed metal.
- Customize the brand name and tagline to reflect your unique value proposition, ensuring the typography colors complement your product\
- ,
- s premium craftsmanship and elegant details.

> Replace monitor screens with custom images using this AI prompt, featuring realistic perspective matching, lighting balance, and professional presentation quality.

### Prompt

```
{
  "task": "minimal_desktop_monitor_screen_replacement",
  "input": {
    "user_uploaded_image": "PLACEHOLDER_FOR_UPLOADED_IMAGE",
    "auto_fit_to_screen": true,
    "preserve_aspect_ratio": true,
    "center_crop_if_needed": true
  },
  "scene": {
    "composition": "[MONITOR SETUP] with two silhouetted people on left and right",
    "camera_angle": "straight-on frontal view",
    "environment": "[BACKGROUND]",
    "foreground": "two human silhouettes seated facing the monitor",
    "vibe": "clean dark mode presentation aesthetic"
  },
  "screen_integration": {
    "replace_existing_screen_content": true,
    "remove_existing_UI_text": true,
    "apply_subtle_perspective_match": true,
    "respect_monitor_bezel_boundaries": true,
    "apply_soft_screen_emission": true,
    "match_screen_brightness_to_backlight": true,
    "avoid_flat_overlay_effect": true
  },
  "lighting": {
    "style": "high contrast backlit studio",
    "background_light": "bright white",
    "foreground_subjects": "dark silhouettes",
    "screen_brightness": "balanced so screen content remains readable",
    "shadow_style": "minimal detail in silhouettes"
  },
  "realism_rules": {
    "maintain_monitor_proportions": true,
    "no_screen_spill_over_bezel": true,
    "preserve_silhouette_edges": true,
    "no_extra_limbs_or_distortion": true,
    "keep_clean_minimal_composition": true
  },
  "output": {
    "style": "ultra clean high-contrast product presentation",
    "resolution": "high resolution",
    "detail_level": "commercial tech mockup quality",
    "no_added_text": true
  }
}
```

### What it does

- Creates an AI image showing a desktop monitor with two silhouetted people viewing it from both sides in a backlit setup.
- Replaces the monitor\
- ,

### Tips

- Upload your screenshot, dashboard, or app interface in high-resolution for the AI image to display it naturally on the monitor screen.
- Choose a background environment that complements your content, such as a modern office for business tools or a creative studio for design software.
- Use the JSON prompt to guide the AI in creating a professional tech presentation scene with realistic screen integration and balanced lighting.

### How to use

1. Step 1: Attach your logo / image.

## 🍽️ Create Minimalist Product Plate Mockups

| Field | Value |
|---|---|

| **Date** | 2026-05-28 |
| **Views** | 56 |
| **Tags** | Image Prompts, Marketing, Content Strategy, Minimalist |

> Create stunning product presentations with this AI prompt, featuring overhead plate compositions with realistic lighting, shadows, and minimalist styling.

### Prompt

```
{
  "project": {
    "title": "Single Plate Conceptual Product Presentation",
    "goal": "Integrate the uploaded product image into a minimalist overhead dinner plate composition without altering the product",
    "language": "en"
  },
  "image_usage": {
    "use_uploaded_product_exactly": true,
    "preserve_shape": true,
    "preserve_label": true,
    "preserve_colors": true,
    "preserve_proportions": true,
    "do_not_generate_new_product": true
  },
  "composition": {
    "camera_angle": "90-degree overhead flat lay",
    "background": "[SURFACE MATERIAL]",
    "layout": "single [TABLEWARE STYLE] plate centered",
    "cutlery": {
      "left": "fork",
      "right": "knife",
      "material": "[TABLEWARE STYLE] matching cutlery"
    },
    "product_placement": {
      "position": "center of plate",
      "scale": "realistic proportion relative to plate",
      "orientation": "natural horizontal or vertical alignment depending on product shape"
    }
  },
  "lighting": {
    "style": "[LIGHTING MOOD]",
    "match_product_lighting": true,
    "contact_shadow": "natural soft shadow under the real product",
    "realistic_reflection_alignment": true
  },
  "visual_style": {
    "ultra_photoreal": true,
    "high_material_accuracy": true,
    "no_fake_placeholder_object": true
  },
  "output": {
    "aspect_ratio": "1:1 or 4:5",
    "resolution": "very high",
    "no_text": true,
    "no_logo_added": true,
    "no_watermark": true
  },
  "negative_prompt": [
    "empty plate",
    "generated bottle",
    "placeholder object",
    "altered product",
    "distorted label",
    "added branding",
    "text overlay"
  ]
}
```

### What it does

- Places an uploaded product image at the center of a dinner plate in a realistic overhead composition.
- Preserves the original product\
- ,

### Tips

- Ensure your product image is high-resolution on transparent background for seamless integration into the plate composition.
- Choose a surface material and tableware style that complement your product\
- ,
- s appeal, like soft natural light for organic goods or dramatic side lighting for premium beverages.

1. Step 1: Attach your logo / image.

## 🌘 Create Monochrome Cinematic Portraits

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| **Type** | Prompts |
| **Tool** | Nano Banana |
| **Output** | Text |
| **Date** | 2026-05-28 |
| **Views** | 29 |
| **Tags** | Photography, Marketing, Content Strategy, Monochrome |
| **Recommended Tools** | Nano Banana |

> Generate stunning portrait photography prompts with this AI prompt, featuring customizable subjects, weather conditions, lighting setups, and cinematic moods for creative projects.

### Prompt

```
{
  "description": "A dramatic black-and-white close-up portrait of a [SUBJECT] standing in the [WEATHER CONDITION].",
  "subject": {
    "gender": "[SUBJECT gender]",
    "pose": "side profile, facing left",
    "expression": "calm and pensive",
    "details": {
      "hair": "long, wavy, wet strands falling forward",
      "skin": "wet with visible [WEATHER CONDITION] droplets",
      "makeup": "soft natural makeup with defined lashes",
      "wardrobe": "sleeveless top (minimal visible)"
    }
  },
  "environment": {
    "weather": "[WEATHER CONDITION] visible in the background",
    "lighting": "soft, moody, directional light creating gentle highlights and shadows",
    "tone": "dark, cinematic, high-contrast monochrome"
  },
  "composition": {
    "shot_type": "close-up portrait",
    "focus": "sharp focus on the [SUBJECT]'s face",
    "background": "blurred, dark, deep bokeh"
  },
  "mood": "[MOOD]"
}
```

### What it does

- Generates a black-and-white AI image portrait showing a subject in side profile during specific weather conditions.
- Creates dramatic lighting with high contrast that highlights wet hair and skin droplets for a cinematic mood.
- Produces a close-up shot with sharp facial focus while keeping the background blurred and dark.

### Tips

- Choose a subject that matches your creative vision, such as a woman, man, or non-binary person, and select a weather condition like rain, snow, or mist that enhances the dramatic mood of your AI image prompt.
- Pick a mood that aligns with your storytelling goals, such as melancholic, contemplative, mysterious, or resilient, to give your AI image emotional depth and narrative purpose.
- Use the JSON prompt to guide the AI in creating a cinematic black-and-white portrait, ensuring the weather condition you select complements the wet hair and skin details for visual consistency.

> Generate stunning beauty campaign visuals with this AI prompt, featuring fashion models posed with oversized products in photorealistic editorial style.

### Prompt

```
{
  "subject": "fashion model leaning against a massively oversized beauty product",
  "character": {
    "gender": "female",
    "age_range": "early 20s",
    "body_type": "slim, athletic",
    "skin_tone": "light natural skin tone",
    "hair": "dark brown hair in a high ponytail with loose front strands",
    "face_structure": "soft jawline, refined nose, expressive eyes",
    "expression": "confident, thoughtful, editorial gaze",
    "pose": "upper body relaxed, elbow resting on product, fingers near lips"
  },
  "wardrobe": {
    "top": "[WARDROBE TOP]",
    "bottom": "[WARDROBE BOTTOM]",
    "socks": "[WARDROBE SOCKS]",
    "shoes": "[WARDROBE SHOES]",
    "style": "[WARDROBE STYLE]"
  },
  "hero_product": {
    "brand": "[PRODUCT BRAND]",
    "product_name": "[PRODUCT NAME]",
    "product_state": "closed, cap attached, realistic retail form",
    "scale": "extreme oversized, towering, significantly larger than the model's torso",
    "relative_size": "[PRODUCT TYPE] height equals or exceeds model shoulder height",
    "design": {
      "form": "[PRODUCT FORM]",
      "cap": "[PRODUCT CAP]",
      "material": "[PRODUCT MATERIAL]",
      "finish": "[PRODUCT FINISH]",
      "color": "[PRODUCT COLOR]",
      "branding": "[BRAND NAME] text clearly visible and correctly proportioned"
    },
    "interaction": "model naturally leans her elbow and forearm on the giant [PRODUCT TYPE] as if it were furniture",
    "restrictions": [
      "no stack",
      "no layered product",
      "no exploded view",
      "no sculptural abstraction",
      "single [PRODUCT TYPE] only"
    ]
  },
  "environment": {
    "location": "[ENVIRONMENT]",
    "background": "[BACKDROP]",
    "floor": "seamless studio floor",
    "vibe": "luxury beauty campaign, minimal and clean"
  },
  "lighting": {
    "type": "soft editorial studio lighting",
    "emphasis": "subtle highlights on model's face and strong specular shine on [PRODUCT TYPE] tube",
    "shadows": "controlled and soft"
  },
  "camera": {
    "shot_type": "medium-close fashion editorial",
    "framing": "model's face and upper body dominant, product still visibly massive",
    "lens": "50mm",
    "focus": "tack-sharp face, sharp product edges"
  },
  "render_style": {
    "photorealism": "very high",
    "priority": "model realism first, product scale second",
    "texture_accuracy": "realistic skin pores, fabric folds, cosmetic plastic reflections"
  },
  "style_tags": [
    "[PRODUCT BRAND] campaign",
    "hero product scale",
    "beauty editorial",
    "model-driven composition",
    "photorealistic",
    "luxury advertising"
  ]
}
```

### What it does

- Generates a photorealistic AI image of a fashion model casually leaning against an oversized beauty product.

- Produces editorial-style lighting that highlights both the model\
- s realistic details.

## 🪜 Create Self-Service Tutorial Scripts

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| **Type** | Prompts |
| **Tool** | ChatGPT |
| **Output** | Text |
| **Date** | 2026-05-28 |
| **Views** | 137 |
| **Tags** | Support, Customer Experience, Tickets, Onboarding |
| **Recommended Tools** | ChatGPT, Gemini, Claude |

> Create professional video tutorial scripts with this AI prompt, including hooks, signposting, voiceover copy, visual cues, mistake callouts, and end screens.

### Prompt

```
# CONTEXT:
Adopt the role of customer education architect. The user's product is bleeding users during onboarding because customers can't figure out how to extract value fast enough. Support tickets pile up with the same questions while trial conversions stagnate. Previous tutorial attempts failed because they documented features instead of teaching outcomes—customers watched passively, then still couldn't execute. The help center exists but nobody uses it because content doesn't match the moment of confusion. Competitors are winning on perceived ease-of-use despite having inferior products. The user needs tutorials that don't just inform but actually transfer capability, embedded at friction points where customers either break through or bounce.

# ROLE:
You're a customer education video producer who spent five years analyzing why some tutorials get 80% watch-through rates while others get abandoned at 12 seconds, discovered that the difference isn't production quality but outcome-clarity and pacing, and now obsessively structures every script around the exact moment a customer thinks "Will this actually help me right now?" Your mission: Design self-service video tutorial scripts that transform confused trial users into competent customers before they churn. Before any action, think step by step: identify the customer's emotional state when they click this tutorial, determine the smallest viable outcome that proves value, map the exact sequence of actions with zero assumed knowledge, flag the one mistake that will derail them, and script the hook that makes them commit the next 3 minutes.

# RESPONSE GUIDELINES:
Each tutorial script should be organized to maximize watch-through and knowledge transfer:

**Hook Section (First 8 seconds)**: State the concrete outcome the viewer will achieve and the time commitment required. This determines whether they stay or abandon. The goal is immediate clarity on value and investment.

**Signpost Structure (2-4 named sections)**: Break the tutorial into clearly labeled steps that allow viewers to skip to relevant parts and track progress. Each section begins with what the viewer will accomplish, not what feature you'll show.

**Voiceover Copy (Full narration)**: Write conversational, word-for-word narration at 130-150 words per minute. Each sentence maps to a specific on-screen action. Include production cues in [brackets] for highlights, zooms, pauses, and visual emphasis.

**On-Screen Text Overlays**: Specify text that reinforces critical instructions—field names, settings, values to enter. These support non-native speakers and sound-off viewing.

**Common Mistake Callout**: Include one "Watch out for this" moment per tutorial that flags a frequent error and shows the correct approach. This creates the highest engagement moment and builds trust.

**End Screen**: Provide a specific next action for the viewer to attempt immediately, followed by a link to the relevant help article for reference.

Each section should include estimated timestamps to keep the final video between 2-4 minutes total.

# TASK CRITERIA:

1. **Outcome-first framing**: Every tutorial opens with what the customer will achieve, not what feature exists. The hook must answer "Why should I invest the next 3 minutes?"

2. **Action-mapped narration**: Every sentence of voiceover corresponds to a visible on-screen action. No abstract explanations without visual anchors.

3. **Assumption-free instruction**: Write for customers with zero prior knowledge. Define terms, show where to click, explain why each step matters.

4. **Pacing precision**: Target 130-150 words per minute. Include [PAUSE] cues where the viewer needs processing time.

5. **Visual direction specificity**: Use [HIGHLIGHT], [ZOOM], [CIRCLE], [ARROW] cues so producers know exactly what to emphasize on screen.

6. **Mistake prevention**: Identify the one error that derails most users and explicitly call it out with the correct alternative.

7. **Concrete next steps**: End screens must give a specific task to attempt, not generic encouragement.

**AVOID:**
- Scripts exceeding 4 minutes (break into series instead)
- Generic openings like "Welcome to this tutorial on..."
- Robotic, manual-reading tone
- Screen recordings without explanatory voiceover
- Feature demonstrations without outcome context
- Assumed technical knowledge
- Vague CTAs like "Try it yourself" without specifics

**FOCUS ON:**
- First 8 seconds determining watch-through
- Matching script to customer's emotional state at moment of need
- Showing the correct path AND the common wrong turn
- Making every second justify the viewer's time investment

# INFORMATION ABOUT ME:
- My product/service: [DESCRIBE YOUR PRODUCT/SERVICE]
- My tutorial topics: [LIST TUTORIAL TOPICS - e.g., "How to set up your account", "How to create your first project", "How to invite team members"]
- My target audience and tech comfort level: [DESCRIBE AUDIENCE AND TECH COMFORT]
- My tutorial access context: [DESCRIBE WHEN/WHY CUSTOMERS ACCESS TUTORIALS - e.g., "during initial setup", "when stuck on a feature"]
- My preferred video style: [SPECIFY STYLE - e.g., "screen recording with voiceover", "animated explainer", "talking head with screen share"]

# RESPONSE FORMAT:
For each tutorial topic, provide a complete script structured as follows:

**TUTORIAL TITLE:** [Clear, outcome-focused title]

**ESTIMATED TOTAL LENGTH:** [X minutes]

---

**HOOK** [0:00-0:08]
[Voiceover text that states outcome and time commitment]
[Visual direction cues in brackets]

---

**SECTION 1: [Descriptive Section Name]** [0:08-X:XX]
[Brief outcome statement for this section]

[Voiceover text]
[Visual cues: HIGHLIGHT, ZOOM, PAUSE, etc.]
[On-screen text overlays where needed]

---

**SECTION 2: [Descriptive Section Name]** [X:XX-X:XX]
[Brief outcome statement for this section]

[Voiceover text]
[Visual cues]
[On-screen text overlays where needed]

---

**[SECTION 3/4 if needed]**

---

**COMMON MISTAKE CALLOUT** [X:XX-X:XX]
[Voiceover text flagging the common error and showing correct approach]
[Visual cues showing both wrong and right way]

---

**END SCREEN** [X:XX-X:XX]
[Voiceover text with specific next action]
[On-screen text with link to help article]

---

Repeat this structure for each tutorial topic provided.
```

### What it does

- Analyzes an AI prompt that creates video tutorial scripts for SaaS products and help centers.
- Explains how the AI prompt guides script writing with hooks, sections, voiceover copy, and visual cues.
- Shows what structure the AI prompt uses to produce engaging tutorial content with high watch-through rates.

### Tips

- Test your AI prompt with a single tutorial first before creating the full series, allowing you to refine the hook structure and pacing based on actual watch-through data from your help center analytics.
- Create a style guide document that captures the tone and visual cues from your first successful script, then reference it when running the AI prompt for subsequent tutorials to maintain consistency across your video library.
- After generating scripts with this AI prompt, have team members from sales or support review them to identify missing troubleshooting steps or real-world scenarios that customers frequently encounter but weren\

---

```
{

    "product": "UPLOAD_PRODUCT_IMAGE_HERE"
  },
  "scene": {
    "environment": "minimal sunlit wall",
    "wall": {
      "color": "[WALL TONE]",
      "texture": "smooth plaster with subtle natural imperfections",
      "grain": "soft film grain"
    },
    "lighting": {
      "type": "warm afternoon sunlight",
      "direction": "side angled light creating elongated shadows",

    "color_restriction": "no colors except natural wall tone and white typography"
  },

      "cap_locked": true,
      "edges_precise": true,
      "proportions_exact": true,
      "silhouette_recreated_from_upload": true
    }
  },
  "label_projection": {
    "source": "label text extracted from uploaded product image",
    "projection_style": "projected onto the product shadow",
    "typography": {
      "color": "clean crisp white",
      "placement_exact": true,
      "spacing_exact": true,
      "size_exact": true,
      "alignment_precise": true
    }
  },
  "quality": {
    "resolution": "ultra high resolution",
    "detail_level": "hyperreal shadow edges and wall texture fidelity",
    "finish": "editorial luxury skincare finish"
  }
}
```

- ,
- ,

### What it does

- Generates a 3×2 grid AI image advertisement showcasing a snack product across six distinct panels with modern food photography.
- Creates vibrant product shots including hero angles, macro textures, floating chips, lifestyle scenes, and ingredient details on colorful backgrounds.
- Produces professional studio-lit AI images with clean shadows and bright compositions perfect for social media and retail marketing campaigns.

### Tips

- Choose a snack product that photographs well and fill in the product name with your actual brand, selecting a color palette that matches your packaging to maintain brand consistency across all six panels.
- Consider the snack type carefully when filling variables, as different products like pretzels, popcorn, or veggie chips will require adjusting the ingredient detail panel and texture close-up to match your specific product characteristics.
- Use the JSON prompt to guide the AI in creating a cohesive 3×2 grid advertisement that balances product shots with lifestyle moments, ensuring your chosen background colors complement rather than compete with your snack packaging design.

### How to use

1. Step 1: Attach your logo / image.

## ♟️ Create Social Media Content Calendars

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| **Type** | Prompts |
| **Tool** | ChatGPT |
| **Output** | Text |
| **Date** | 2026-05-28 |
| **Views** | 161 |
| **Tags** | Campaigns, Social Media, Content Strategy, Opportunity Analysis |
| **Recommended Tools** | ChatGPT, Gemini, Claude |

> Create 30-day social media content calendars with this AI prompt, including daily post ideas, formats, and engagement goals for your niche.

### Prompt

```
Adopt the role of an expert social media strategist and content architect who has spent a decade building viral campaigns and sustainable content ecosystems for brands across every major platform. Your primary objective is to design a comprehensive 30-day content calendar that strategically balances audience growth, community engagement, and conversion optimization in a detailed, actionable format. You understand that effective content calendars aren't just lists of posts—they're strategic narratives that build momentum, establish authority, and guide audiences through intentional journeys from awareness to action. Analyze the user's niche to identify content pillars, audience pain points, platform-specific best practices, and optimal posting rhythms. Structure the calendar to create thematic coherence across the month while maintaining daily variety that prevents audience fatigue. Each piece of content should serve a specific strategic purpose within the larger conversion funnel, whether that's building trust, demonstrating expertise, fostering community, or driving action. Consider platform algorithms, engagement patterns, content fatigue cycles, and the psychological progression audiences need to move from strangers to engaged community members. Take a deep breath and work on this problem step-by-step.

Begin by identifying 3-5 core content pillars that align with the niche and audience needs. Map out a strategic flow across the 30 days that builds narrative momentum rather than random posts. For each day, specify the exact post concept, the recommended format optimized for maximum platform performance, the primary goal it serves in the marketing funnel, suggested hooks or angles to maximize engagement, and how it connects to the broader monthly narrative. Include a strategic mix of educational content, entertainment, community-building posts, social proof, and conversion-focused content in proportions appropriate to the niche. Incorporate platform-specific best practices for timing, format selection, and engagement optimization. Design the calendar so posts build on each other, creating anticipation and narrative threads that keep audiences returning. Include notes on repurposing opportunities and cross-platform adaptation strategies to maximize content ROI.

#INFORMATION ABOUT ME:
My niche/industry: [INSERT YOUR NICHE OR INDUSTRY]
My target audience: [INSERT YOUR TARGET AUDIENCE DETAILS]
My primary social media platforms: [INSERT YOUR MAIN PLATFORMS]
My main content goals: [INSERT YOUR PRIMARY GOALS - AWARENESS/ENGAGEMENT/LEADS/SALES]
My unique value proposition: [INSERT WHAT MAKES YOU DIFFERENT IN YOUR NICHE]

MOST IMPORTANT!: Your output must be in a comprehensive markdown table format with columns including Day, Content Theme, Post Concept, Format Type, Primary Goal, Key Hook/Angle, and Strategic Notes. Use clear section breaks for each week and include a brief strategic overview at the beginning explaining the monthly narrative arc.
```

### What it does

- Creates a month-long social media content calendar tailored to your specific niche.
- Generates daily post ideas with format suggestions like carousels, reels, and threads.
- Assigns clear goals to each post focusing on awareness, engagement, or lead generation.

### Tips

- Review your existing content performance metrics before implementing the 30-day calendar to identify which post types and topics resonate most with your audience, allowing you to adjust the AI prompt suggestions based on real data.
- Schedule specific time blocks each week to batch-create content for multiple days at once, using the calendar as your roadmap to maintain consistency and reduce the daily pressure of content creation.
- Track which posts from the calendar generate the most leads or engagement, then ask the AI prompt to create variations of those high-performing concepts for future months to build on your success.

```
      "lighting"
```

> Design automated win-back campaigns with this AI prompt, including churn segment analysis, reactivation sequences, offer strategies, and conversion tracking.

### Prompt

```
Create automated win-back campaigns by churn segment.

For each segment include:
- Likely churn reason
- Message sequence
- Offer strategy
- Channel cadence
- Stop/send suppression rules

Add KPIs: reactivation rate, retained revenue, unsubscribes.

# INFORMATION ABOUT ME:
- My churned user segments: [INSERT]
- My acceptable offer limits: [INSERT]
- My channels: [INSERT]
- My historical win-back performance: [INSERT IF AVAILABLE]
```

### What it does

- Builds segmented reactivation journeys for churned customers.
- Aligns offers and messaging to churn drivers.
- Prevents over-messaging with suppression logic.

### Tips

- Exclude users with unresolved critical support issues.
- Test one variable per segment at a time.
- Track long-term retention after reactivation, not just initial return.

### How to use

1. Provide churn segments, offers, and channel constraints.
2. Run prompt and deploy journeys in your campaign automation stack.
